1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ u d+h+wa dza Ta/ ma hA kalpa ma hA/ bo dI sa ta ba kurbA Na pa tra la bi sa ra ta bA
1b2(rgyud): ga ba tI/ Ar+ya tA rA/ mu la kal+la na ma/ bod skad du/ ral pa gye na rjes kyi rtog pa chen po/ byang chub
1b3(rgyud): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'o/ rnam par 'phrul pa le'u rab 'byam las/ bcom ldan 'das ma
1b4(rgyud): 'phags ma sgrol ma'i rtsa ba'i rtog pa zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal
1b5(rgyud): lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i ngas gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ma 'phags ma sgrol ma'i grwa'i
2a1(rgyud): steng byi nam mkha'i dkyil na rab tu bzhugs te/ ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba/ bsam gyis mi khyab pas rab tu phye ba'i byang chub
2a2(rgyud): sems dpa' 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor dang ldan par bzhugs so// de la bcom ldan 'das kyis gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu
2a3(rgyud): rnams la bka' spel pa/ lha'i bu khyed rnams nyon ngas cig/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ spyan ras
2a4(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug gi rmad du byung ba'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i cho 'phrul gyi spyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi
2a5(rgyud): par rnam par thar pa'i dkyil 'khor byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa sems can thams cad nye bar 'tshe bar byed pa/ tshong
2a6(rgyud): nad med pa dang / dbang phyug dang / yid kyi shing rta yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i rigs sngags dang / gsang sngags kyi bzhi
2b1(rgyud): sems can thams cad la phan pa'i ched du bshad kyis/ de legs par nyon la legs par yid la gyis shig/ ngas bshad do
2b2(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das la legs so zhes so// de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de rnams thal mo sbyar ba btud nas
2b3(rgyud): 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi spyod pa ting nge 'dzin
2b4(rgyud): gyi khyad par/ so sor thob par byed pa rdo rje bo na gnon par byed pa/ bdud 'dul bar byed pa/ chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu
2b5(rgyud): skor bar byed pa/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad nges par 'byung bar byed pa/ lha dang mi rnams su skye bar byed pa/ sdug bsngal
2b6(rgyud): thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa/ dbul ba dang / nad kyis btab pa thams cad kyi nad sel bar byed pa nyid dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten
3a1(rgyud): sa su sgyu sa blugs/ spyod pa dis rgyas pa smra / ma
3a2(rgyud): cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa de gsung du gsol/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni don med par gsung bar byed pa ma lags na/ bcom
3a3(rgyud): ldan 'das byams pa'i sems dang / bdag cag dang sems can thams cad la rjes su rtse bar nye bar bzung nas de gsung du gsol// 
3a4(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po la sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyis
3a5(rgyud): rnam par gzigs nas/ rnam par dag pa'i yul la 'od zer rnam par 'phro ba/ rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhun
3a6(rgyud): so// snyoms par bzhugs ma thag tu bcom ldan 'das kyi mdzod spu nas/ me tog lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kun tu bskul bar byed pa
3a7(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i 'od zer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gis yongs su bskor ba nyid kyis bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ stong gsum
3b1(rgyud): gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas pa 'das pa nas/ nub phyogs kyi char gang ga'i klung gi brgya stong phrag gi bye ma snyed dang mnyam po'i 'jig rten
3b2(rgyud): byi khams las 'das pa na/ bde ba can zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams su rjes su zhugs te gang du de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med bzhugs pa der
3b3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug kyang sngon gyi smon lam gyi dbang gis byang chub sems dpa' chen po'i spyod pa la
3b4(rgyud): so sor gnas pa rnams kyi thabs gcig tu bzhug/ pa de 'od zer gyi snang ba mthong bas cung zad rab tu bshad zhal de nyid kyis byang chub sems
3b5(rgyud): dpa'i tshogs la bka' stsal to// kye rgyal ba'i sras rnams/ 'di ni bdag cag rnams kun du skul bar byed pa'i 'dir 'ongs pa yin pa khyed cag gis
3b6(rgyud): shes par gyis shig/ de nas yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams spyan gdangs nas/ 'di'i 'od zer gyi snang ba gang yin pa der mngon
3b7(rgyud): par phyogs te gnas so// de nas kun du skul bar byed pa 'od zer des bde ba can gyi 'jig rten gyi khams chen po kun du snang bas kun nas snang bar byas nas
4a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs
4a2(rgyud): kyi ye shes kyi spyi bor nub par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bstan las langs nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag
4a3(rgyud): maud la lan gsum skor ba byas nas mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
4a4(rgyud): ldan 'das dgongs su gsol// bdag cag bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa grang
4a5(rgyud): na ba der song ste/ bcom ldan 'das kyis mi 'jed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams de dang / bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la lta ba dang / phyag 'tshal zhing snyen bkure ba dang / rig
4a6(rgyud): sngags dang / gsang sngags thams cad kyi spyod pa dang / sgrub thabs kyi cho ga dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i rtog pa dang / gsang ba'i ris ris kyi cho ga dang / zlas pa dang / rig pa'i
4a7(rgyud): dbang skur pa thams cad khyad par stan dus sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par 'tshal lo/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
4a8(rgyud): pa 'od dpag med pas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// sems dpa' chen po gang de lta de'i dus la brab par na song cig/ nga'i tshig
4b1(rgyud): gis kyang bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la gnod pa chung ngam/ nyams pa chung ba'am/ ldang ba yang ngam/ reg par gnas sam/ zhes sbed par bya'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das ni
4b2(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag tu med pas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ sems dpa' chen po gang ga'i
4b3(rgyud): klu brgya stong phrag gi bye ma la sogs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang khyod kyi rigs dang / gsang sngags kyi spyod pa dang / dkyil
4b4(rgyud): 'khor gyi rtog pa dang / gsang ba'i dbang skur ba dang / phyag rgya dang / ras ris kyi cho ga dang / spyan bsreg dang / bzlas pa'i nges pa bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs
4b5(rgyud): par byed pa/ sems can thams cad kun nas dag par byed pa rin po che snang ba'i le'u rab 'byom 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i ye shes rnams kyis rig
4b6(rgyud): sngags dang / gsang sngags la 'jug par byed pa/ ston pa mthar thug par zin pa/ nang gi dus dang ldan pa dang / dam tshig rab 'jam gyi le'u dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las
4b7(rgyud): 'das pa mtha' dag ma dag ma lus per sdus pa/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / 'phags pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa la/ 
4b8(rgyud): zhugs pa dang / spyod pa mthar thug par gsungs pa dang ldan pa dag gsungs pa la yang 'di la rjes su yid rang ba kho na'o// sems dpa' chen po// da lA de'i dus la bab par shes khyad sa / 
5a1(rgyud): shAkya thub pa'i drung du de la mngon du phyogs pas dam pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di nyon la khyod kyang smra bar 'gyur ro// 'di la yang rtsa ba'i rig sngags su 'gyur ba ni/ na mo rang
5a2(rgyud): na tra yA ya/ na mo a mi tA b+ha ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ a ra ha te samya kaM b+hud dA ya/ na mo ar+ya a ba lo ki te sha ra ya/ bo d+hi sa twA ya/ ma hA sa twA ya/ na mo byA gA t+yai/ aR+ya ta ra ye/ bo d+hi sa ta yai/ ma hA
5a3(rgyud): sa twa ye/ tad+ya thA/ ta re rI dzi kA d+har+m+ma nir+ye te/ ta re tud tA ro/ shA tA d+harmaM naur+ya te/ tA re a ne bI lA r+ya/ d+harma nir+ya te/ tud ta re/ tu re tu re tu hi ni/ tra sa ni pi tr-i sa nI/ o hA nI ma hA ni/ dza ma b+ha ni snam
5a4(rgyud): pa ni pra b+he nA pa b+hi/ ti li ti li/ tsa li tsi li/ be ga sA maM ni kun NI ku NI/ ma hA ku NA/ d+ha ra d+ha ra/ b+ha na pa ta hu ru hU ru/ ku ru ku ru/ a haM yA yA/ tsin+ta yA mi tsin+ta ya taM mi ku ru swa dA yA
5a5(rgyud): swA hA// / 'di ni sems dpa' chen po khyod kyi 'phags mi sgrol ma'i rtsa ba'i rig pa yin te/ de bzhin gshogapa thams cad kyi snying po'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
5a6(rgyud): thams cad kyis shing gsungs par 'gyur ba ste/ khyod kyis kyang de lta smra bar 'gyur ro// mi 'jeng gi 'jig rten gyi khams dring rgyas pas rnam par phye ba'i mthar shAkya thub pa byon te/ shAkya thub pas
5a7(rgyud): rjes su gnang ba'o// 'di la mchog gi snying por 'gyur ba yang // na mo rang na tu sA yA/ na mo ar+ya ba lo ki ti shwa rA ya/ bo d+hi sa ta ya/ mahA sa ta ya/ ta re tu ta re tu te ra swA hA// / 'di la nye ba'i
5a8(rgyud): snying po'o// na mo rad na tA ya yA/ na maHsarba bud d+ha bu d+hi sa ta naM/ a ku ru ku ru le swA hA/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug bcom
5b1(rgyud): ldan 'das kyis rjes su gnang nas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyu 'thun pa/ byang chub kyi snying po kun du thob par byed pa/ thams cad kyi bkod pa'i brgyan zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
5b2(rgyud): snyoms par bzhugs so// snyoms par bzhugs ma thag tu phyogs bzhi rnams dang / steng dang 'og dang / zad ka'i mthar thug pa thams cad du thams cad dang ldan pa'i phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi
5b3(rgyud): khams su rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis kun du gang bar gyur to// rgyal ba'i sras po legs so legs so// gang khyod ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par 'di lta bu la snyoms
5b4(rgyud): par zhugs pa ni/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mi nus te/ byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa la rab tu bzhugs pas/ sa bcu la rab tu bzhugs pa rnams kyis kyang
5b5(rgyud): snyoms par 'jug par mi nus so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de rnams kyis thabs gcig byams pa
5b6(rgyud): dang bcas pa/ bcom ldan 'das 'phags ma sgrol ma'i mchog gi snying po mchog tu gsang ba/ don thams cad sgrub par byed pa yi go gcig pa zhes bya ba/ mchog tu gsang ba'i sems can thams
5b7(rgyud): cad kyi las thams cad byed ma/ rig sngags gzhan rnams kyis kyang / rig sngags dang gsang sngags kyi spyod pa'i khyad par sgrub par byed pa dang / 'thun pa'i rig sngags gsung bar gyur to// de nas
5b8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tsha dpag med yud tsam zhig ci yang mi gsung bar 'gyur to// thams cad du thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten la sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyis kan du gzig
6a1(rgyud): nas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dgongs pa/ byams pa'i bdag nyid kyi sems kyi rig sngags gsungs par gyur to// na mo sarba bu d+ha naM/ oM gIH'di ni bcom ldan
6a2(rgyud): 'das ma'i mchog gi snying po las thams cad byed pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas 'di lta ste/ skyes bu stobs
6a3(rgyud): dang ldan pa zhes bya ba lag pa skum pa las byung ba 'am/ rkyang ba las skum pa dang / se gol rtog pa tsam gyis dang / mig 'byed 'dzum sam skad cig tsam gyi ting nge 'dzin/ rdzu 'phrul gyi spongs
6a4(rgyud): 'phyogs pa'i blo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par rnam pa re 'phrul pa nyid ces bya ba la snyoms par bzhugasate/ mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams su 'ongs kyang slad 'khod do/ 
6a5(rgyud): steng gi nam mkha'i 'thil du nor bu rin po chen po la so sor 'khod pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po slar 'khod nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'od
6a6(rgyud): zer chen po kun du snang bas kun du snang bar byas nas/ rin po che snang ba'i bdag po'i rgyan gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs par gyur to// byang chub sems
6a7(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu khang partsigs pa rin po che du mas rnam par phye ba dang / rin po che'i gdugs du mas dpag tshad
6a8(rgyud): brgya stong phrag du khyab pa dang / lha'i gos dang / dar gyi brgyan gyis nye bar mdzes par spras pa dang / lha'i me tog dang / ba dan dang / rgyal mtshan dang / phreng ba dang / rin po cho g.yer kha'i dra ba bcings pa
6b1(rgyud): sgra snyan pa 'khrol ba 'jug pa dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa' so sor gnas par byed pa lha'i dri dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma'i char 'bebs par byed pa mngon par sprul te/ bcom ldan 'das
6b2(rgyud): shAkya thub pa la mchod pa'i las byed do// ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i tshe 'phrul byang chub sems dpa'i rnam 'phrul mthong ngo // de nas gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de rnams dga' ba dang bcas pas/ sru zing
6b3(rgyud): zhes byed do// lha'i gnas rnams thams cad rab tu g.yo ba dang ldan pa mthong nas skrag cing snying 'dar te 'on te 'byor pa yongs nyams sam/ ci zhes phan tshun rings thabs su skad 'thon pos smra ba brtsom
6b4(rgyud): zhes 'di skad ces kyang smras so// bcom ldan 'das yongs su skyobs shig/ shAkya thub pa yongasu skye bas shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis thams cad dang ldan pa'i lha'i 'khor la
6b5(rgyud): bka' stsal to// ma 'jigs shig 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing kun
6b6(rgyud): nasnga me tog can lta bu nas nga nyid lnga ba dang / phyag 'tshal zhing snyen bkur byed par 'dod te/ don chen po'i spyod pa dang / rig sngags kyi tshig dang / chos kyi tshig rmang du byung ba yangs pa nges par bstan pa'i
6b7(rgyud): phyir 'ongs pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mig mi 'dzum par ltas te/ zhabs gnyis la btid nas yi ge tshig rab tu smras pa
6b8(rgyud): 'di rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la mngon par stod do// phyag 'tshal skyes bu mkhyen khyod la/ phyag 'tshal skyes bu mchog khyod la/ spyod pa'i don kun sgrub pa po/ phyag 'tshal skyes bu rtso khyod la/ 
7a1(rgyud): don med thams cad zlog pa po// phyag 'tshal skyes bu seng ge khyod// ngan 'gro thams cad 'joms pa po// dpa' bo chen po khyod phyag 'tshal// bsod nams dri ni mtha' yas pa// phyag 'tshal
7a2(rgyud): skyes bu pad dkar khyod// srid gsum 'dab ni rnam sbyong ba// phyag 'tshal skyes bu pad mu khyod// sdug bsngal thams cad rnam grol byed// thams cad grol khyod phyag 'tshal lo// gdung ba thams cad legs 'dul
7a3(rgyud): byed// zhi ba khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// sngags kyi spyod don sgrub pa po// thams cad grub khyod phyag 'tshal lo// bkra shis kun gyis bkra shis pa// bkra shis khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// chos rnams thams cad kun du
7a4(rgyud): rtogs// sangs rgyas dam tshig khyod phyag 'tshal// chos rnams kun gyi de bzhin nyid// spros pa med pa'i rnam pa ni// yang dag rjes 'jug ston pa po// de bzhin gshegs pa khyod phyag 'tshal// shes dang
7a5(rgyud): shes bya'i dngos po kun// legs par byas shing yang dag thos theg gsum lam dang myang 'das lam// rab tu gnas 'jug rab gnas pa// kun mkhyen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// zhes yi
7a6(rgyud): ge'i tshig rab tu smras pa// 'di rnams kyis bstod pa'i tshig gis bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar mngon par spyod nas 'di skad ces kyang gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di nas gang ga'i klung brgya stong phrag
7a7(rgyud): gi bye ma dang / mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'das nas nub phyogs kyi char kun nas me tog ldan zhes bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du gyur pa der bde ba can zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang na/ 
7a8(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan po// bde bar gshegs pa 'jig rten mkhyen pa bla na med pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ lha dang mi
7b1(rgyud): rnams kyi ston pa/ tshe dpag tu med pa bzhugs te/ des chos ston par mdzad pa ni/ thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba/ don bzang po tshig 'bru bzang po ma 'dres pa/ yongs su rdzogasu pa yongasu
7b2(rgyud): dag pa yongasu byung ba tshangs par spyod pa yang dag par ston par mdzad cing // de 'di ltar bzhugs te/ 'tsho zhing bzhes la chos kyang ston par mdzad do// rig sngags dang gsang sngags kyi don gyi spyod pa rnams
7b3(rgyud): dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod dang / lam gsum gyi spyod pa'i rjes su 'jug pa'i lam dang / skyob pa dang / gnas dang / skyabs dang / dpung gnyen dang / bde ba dang / shin du mthar thug pa dang / shin du yongasu
7b4(rgyud): mthar gtugs pas/ sems can thams cad la ston te/ bcom ldan 'das de nyid kyi mdzad pas rjes su gnang nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyi drung dang nye ba 'dir 'ongs te/ bcom
7b5(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med de/ bcom ldan 'das la gnod pa chung ngam/ nyam nga ba chung ngam ldang ba yang ngam/ snyung ba mi mnga' 'am/ bde ba la reg par gnas sa
7b6(rgyud): zhes yongs su 'dri bar byed de// 'di skad ces gsungs so// gang rnam pa 'di lta bu'i snyigs ma'i dus gang du bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i sku de yang ches ston par mdzad cing rjes su rtogs par bya ba
7b7(rgyud): skye bo la lam gsum gyis byang grol dang lha dang mi rnams kyi skye ba rnyed par mdzad pa de ni ngo mtshar to// bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i sku de brtson 'grus kyis gang du skal ba med pa'i sems can gyi
7b8(rgyud): tshigs srid pa gsum yang dag par 'joms pa'i lam du mthar thug pa/ 'jug par byed pa gtan du grub pa dang / bde ba'i rjes su 'thun pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la/ sems can rnams rab tu bgod
8a1(rgyud): par mdzad pa ni ngo mtshar ro// bcom ldan 'das 'on kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kho nas mkhyen gyis/ bdag gis sangs rgyas
8a2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa rnams// sangs rgyas kyi rnam 'phrul du shes par 'dod pa 'am/ thugs kyi spyod pa la rab tu 'jug
8a3(rgyud): pa'i bsgrub pa dang / sems dpa' shes par 'dod pa 'am/ sems dpa' shes par 'dod pa'am/ mtha' dag nges par ston pa ni bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag rnams kyis kyang brjod par
8a4(rgyud): yang ga le nus// gang yang de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams sgrub bsdus pa dang / so so ba ma lus pa'i ngo bo 'dus ma byas pa'i chos nyid du lwa bA
8a5(rgyud): bya ste/ mthing bas spong bar bya ba spong ba dang / ri por mi thogs pa spyod pa smra bar 'dod pa 'am/ yon tan ston 'dod pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa bcom ldan 'das kho nas 'di
8a6(rgyud): mkhyen gyis/ bdag gis ni yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis rdzu 'phrul pa sprul te/ rin po che chen po'i pad ma la bcom ldan 'das shAkya
8a7(rgyud): thub pa la lha bzhin du bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i
8a8(rgyud): gtam gyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtam gyis mthar gyis dri ba sngon du 'gro ba/ phan tshun chos bstan pa'i mthar rigs kyi/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sgrub pa'i 'dzin du nye bar chom

26a1(rgyud): sgrol mas non pa la bos par gyur to// kye kye khro bo chen po// sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad 'dus pa 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi chen po 'dus pa 'di yi sems can thams cad srungs shig

29b1(rgyud): gsum zhes bya ba brtson 'grus chen pos don thams cad sgrub par byed pa'i khro bo'i rgyal po chen po'o// de gang zhe na/ oM a hUM/ 'di ni khro bo chen po de'i snying po las thams cad pa ste/ dkyil 'khor thams cad
29b2(rgyud): dang / gsang sngags thams cad spyod pa rnams la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos nges par bstan te/ bgegs thams cad 'jig par 'byed pa'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
29b3(rgyud): chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis phyag g.yas pa bteg nas khro ba'i spyi bor bzhag ste/ 'di skad ces smras so// sangs rgyas thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgongs
29b4(rgyud): gsol// gang la la phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khas na rnam par gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mtha' yas shing mu med pa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang ldan pa rnams dam tshig la lhag par gnas

29b8(rgyud): slar yang/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la gzigs nas sems can khyed cag thams cad nyon cig/ gang yang nga'i dam tshig 'di las 'das par byed pa de la khro bo'i rgyal pos tshar gcod par 'gyur te/ gang gi phyir na sangs
30a1(rgyud): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dam tshig ni 'dul bar bya ba ma yin pa'i phyir ro// rig sngags dang gsang sngags kyi don gyi tshig gsang chen ji ltar/ byang chub sems dpa' rdzu 'phrul chen po dang
30a2(rgyud): ldan pa rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin nges par bstan pa 'chad par byed do// de legs par nyon la legs par yid la zung shig dang ngas bshad do// nu mo rang na tra yA ya/ na mo a ni drA d+hA yA/ ta thA ga ta ya/ a ra
30a3(rgyud): ha te/ se myasa? sam bu d+ha ya/ na mo ar+ya a ba lo ki sha rA ya/ bo d+hi sa ta yA/ na mo ba ga wa t+yaM/ ar+yA ta ra yai/ bo tA sa twa yai/ ma hA sa twA yai/ tad+ya thA/ raM dzu ka dzArma/ ni da yA te/ hA re tA re tu dat+ta re/

30a8(rgyud): rgyas mngon sum du mthong ba bzhin du nye bar gnas pa/ rang nyid nga'i grogs po byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir/ mchog tu gsang ba'i rig sngags kyi ngo bos te
30b1(rgyud): bar gnas pa/ bsam pa thams cad yongasu rdzogs par byed pa/ gang dang gang dran pa nyid kyis las thams cad mthar byed pa/ 'jigs chen po rnams yongasu sbyong bar byed pa ste/ bzlas pas lta smos kyang
30b2(rgyud): ci dgos/ de gang zhe na/ na mo rad na tra yA ya/ na mo ar+yA pa lo ki te sha rA ya/ bo d+hi sa twA ya/ ma hA sa twA ya/ ta re tu tA re swa hA/ phyag rgya yang 'dir u ta pa le zhes kyang / rnam par grags pa long spyod thams cad

30b7(rgyud): bA la/ b+hU Shi ta/ pra bo d+hi na/ A yA ni b+ha ga ba ti/ kri ga u tA la d+hi ra Ni/ ma ma shrad+hA yA/ tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha/ sa ma ya nu s+pha ra/ a tra ti ha ha shA sa na tI/ ma bi la mA/ ku ru ku ru phaT swaihA/ 'di ni bcom ldan 'das ma spyan
30b8(rgyud): drang ba'i rig sngags te/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang / 'phags pa nyan thos dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin pa dang / dri za dang / lham
31a1(rgyud): yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / sha za dang / srin po dang / 'byung po thams cad kyi'ang ma yin no// tsan dan gyi tshul lan bdun mngon par sngags pa byas te/ 
31a2(rgyud): phyogs bzhi dang / de bzhin du steng dang / 'og dang / thad ka thams cad du gtor bar bya'o// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / bcom ldan 'das ma sgrol ma dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das
31a3(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi'ang gsang sngags 'di yin te/ 'byung po'i tshogs thams cad dang / sems can thams cad kyang 'ong bar 'gyur ro// / na maHsarba bud+hA naM/ a tra ti ha sha sA nA nAM/ oM d+hu ra d+hu ra/ b+hUm bA si ni/ ma mA rI Shi hU~M/ 
31a4(rgyud): taSh+Tha sa ma ya nu sma ra swA hA/ bdug pa'i rig sngags te/ tsan na na dang / gur gum dang / ga bur gcig tu byas nas/ bdug pa phul bar bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
31a5(rgyud): thams cad byin pa rnams spyod kyi bdug pas/ yid tshim nas zhugs par 'gyur ro// 'dir phyag rgyar gyur pa yang pad ma'i phreng ba grags pa sems can thams cad 'gugs cing zhi ba ste/ spyan pa'i rig
31a6(rgyud): sngags la yang phyag rgya pad ma'i phreng ba bzang po 'di nyid do// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / sems can thams cad byon pa la yang mchod yon dbul bar bya ste/ ga bur dang / tsan dan dang / gur gum
31a7(rgyud): chu dang sbyar nas dzA ti'i me tog dang / mA li ka gsar pa dang / dbyar gyi me tog dang / phun nA ka dang / ba ku la dang / rgya spos rnams te 'di dag gang yang rung ba'i me tog gam/ dus ji lta ba'i me tog gam/ dri bzang po'i me tog
31a8(rgyud): nams dang / bsres nas sngags 'dis mchod yon dbul bar bya'o// na maHsa rba bud+hA naM/ a tre ti hi ta na sha sA naM/ tad+ya nA/ he he ma ma ku ru ni/ ka bi sha ru pa dA rI Ni a na pra tits+tsha pra tits+tsha ma sa ma ya ma nu s+pha ra/ taSh+Tha na
31b1(rgyud): mad+h+ya pra pe sha ya/ pra pi sha sarba b+hu te/ a mu kaM pa ka g+hah+ma g+hAhA am+bA ra bi tsi ri ni swa hA// phyag rgya'i 'dir gang ba zhes grags te/ sems can thams cad kyi rje su 'jug cing brtan pa'o// 'dir dra'i rig sngags su 'gyur ba
31b2(rgyud): yang / na maHsarba pU d+hA nAM/ na maHsa man+ta gAn gAn d+ha/ e b+he/ Sha sha ri ye/ ta thA ga ta ya/ tad+ya thA/ gan dwe gan+d+he/ gan+d+ha na mo ra ma tra tri tsha pra tI tsa tsha de/ gan+d+ha sa ma tA nu tsa ri ni swa hA/ 'dir phyag rgyar 'gyur pa yang / la ma
31b3(rgyud): zhes bya ba bsams pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'o// 'dir me tig gi rig sngags su 'gyur ba yang / na maHsarba bud d+ha bo d+hi si to naM/ a pri ta ha ta sha sa na na/ na maHsaM ka sa mi ta ra dza s+ya/ ta thA ga ta s+ya/ 
31b4(rgyud): tad+ya thA/ ku su me ku su me/ ku su mA g+ho/ ku su ma pu ra bA si ni/ ku su mA ba ti swa hA// / bdag pa'i sngags 'di nyid kyis sngar bshad pa'i bdug par bya'o// rmed byung bsam mi khyab pa'i gsung / sangs rgyas
31b5(rgyud): kun la phyag byas nas/ yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas gsungs pa'i/ gtor ma'i rig sngags rab 'chad byed/ na maHsarba bud d+ha po d+hi sa twA naM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa nA nAM/ tad+ya thA/ he te b+ha ga ba ti/ ma hA sa te/ 
31b6(rgyud): sarba bu b+hA a ba lo ki ti mi bi la mA i ti ba laM gr-in+d+ra pa ya gr-ih+Na hUM hUM hUM hUM/ sarba ta ra phaT swA hA/ lha bshos kyang 'dis dbul bar bya ste/ 'byung po thams cad ma'i gtor mar 'gyur ro// 'di yang phyag rgya ni dbyug pa ste badrin/ 
31b7(rgyud): pa thams cad bzlog par byed pa'o// / na maHsarba bud d+ha bo d+hi sa tI nai/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa nA nAM/ sarba ta mo am+b+ha ka ra bi d+ho/ si tA naM/ na maHsarba sa man+ta dz+yo ti gan+d+ha/ b+ha sa sI yA ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ tad+ya thA/ ha te b+ha ga bA/ 
31b8(rgyud): na dze te ri sI sha ta sa ha sra/ pra ti min+na ta shi rI ra/ bi kur ba bi kur ba/ ma~M hA bo d+hi sa twa sa man+ta/ dz+wa lo do ya ta ta mu d+hi/ khu d+ha khu d+ha/ a ba lo ka ya/ a ba la~M ka ya~M/ mnA la~M sarba sa twA na~M swa hA/ mar me'i rig sngags te/ 
32a1(rgyud): 'dir mar me dbul bar bya'o// phyag rgya ni kha phye ba sems can thams cad rnam par snang bar byed pa'o// na moHsa man ta bud d+ha nAM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa na na~M/ tad+ya thA/ dz+wa la dz+wa la/ dz+wa la dz+wa la/ tu b+hi bo d+ha ka
32a2(rgyud): ha/ ritriSh+Tha na paM ga la/ me'i bya ba byed pa'i rig sngags su 'gyur ro// 'dir yang phyag na kha sbyar zhes par 'jig rten grags/ sems can kun 'od gyis gsal byed/ byang chub sems dpa' bo ldan dang / thu
32a3(rgyud): pa mchog gis mngon gsungs pa'o// de nas yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis/ byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rje la smras pa// gsang ba'i bdag po sngags
32a4(rgyud): 'di ni gsang chen dang bcas shing mchog gis mngon gsungs pa'ide nas yang byang chub sems tu gsang ba yin te/ bu khyod la phan drag po'i mtha'/ mi zad pa'i rigs su grags/ sngags rnams

32a6(rgyud): sarba bud d+ha bi d+hi sa tA naM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa nA nA~M// a~M ka ra ka ra/ ku ru ku ru/ ma ma ka d+yaM/ dzA b+ha dAM sarba ha da ha/ sarba badz+ri bi nI sa~M ka/ mU d+hA da ka dzI ban+ti ta ka ra ma hA pi tI ti ru'i ning/ tsa ba tsa sarba duSh+Ti ma hA gaN+Di
32a7(rgyud): ti dzA b+hin+ta ta ka ra ban+d+ha/ sarba gra ha/ Shag mu kha/ shan+ta bu dza Sha ge tse ra na rA twa mA ga na ya/ baSh+Ta ma na ya/ bra hA d+yaM de ba nA na yAM ba la ma sha bi lam bai la b+hu Sha hriHman+ta la ma d+he pra sha ba ye/ sa ma ya ma nu s+pha ra

32b1(rgyud): glags pa tsam gyis byang chub sems dpa' sa bcu la gnas pa'i dbang phyug rnams kyang rnam par 'jig par byed na/ ma rungs pa'i dgegs rnams lta ci smos// 'di glags pa tsam
32b2(rgyud): gyis bsrung ba chen po byas par 'gyur ro// 'dir phyag rgya 'di yang rigs chen po zhes bya bar gyur te/ bgegs thams cad rnam par byed pa'i khro bo'i rgyal po 'di nyid kyi snying po ni// oM hriHSh+T+r-i'i
32b3(rgyud): kr-i tAM/ nan hUM sarba shr-i truM/ tAm+b+ha ya phaT phaT sa twa/ sngags 'dis dgra thams cad la gzer chen po'i nad dang / yang na rims nyin bzhis zin par 'gyur ro// rtag tu bzlas pas ji srid snang bar byams pa nyid

32b6(rgyud): chen po yang sbyar bar bya'o// bdug pa thams cad la gang 'dod pa de byed par 'gyur ro// mchog gi snying po sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ yi ge gcig pa zhes bya ba ni hUM/ 'di ni las thams
32b7(rgyud): cad pa ste/ phyag rgya mdung chen po yang sbyar bar bya'o// phung khrol thams cad bzlog par byed pa/ 'byung po thams cad dbang du byed pa ste/ mdor na khro bo'i rgyal po 'di ni/ las thams cad la rab tu sbyar bar
32b8(rgyud): bya'o// dkyil 'khor gyi dbus su bzlos pas/ grub pa'i dus su yang khyad par du 'gyur ro// gsheg su gsol ba'i sngags su gyur pa yang / na maHsarba bud d+ha naM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa nA nAM/ tad+ya thA/ dza ya dza yA
33a1(rgyud): su dza ya ma hA ke ru na ka/ bi shwa rU pi ni/ gats+tsha gats+tsha swa b+hA ba ba naM/ sarba bu d+ha swa bis rdza ya sa pa rI bA rAM/ swa b+hA ba naM/ tsa nu pra pa she sa ya/ sa ma ya ma nu sma ra/ sarbaHsha mi si d+h+ya~M tu/ bi d+yaM pa dang ma no
33a2(rgyud): ra tha ma me pa ri bA ra ya swA hA// 'di ni gshegs su gsol ba'i sngags te/ las thams ca dang la sbyar bar bya'o// phyag rgya bzang po'i gdan zhes grags pa ste/ 'dis gdan yang sbyin par bya'o// yid kyis
33a3(rgyud): lan bdun bzlas pas thams cad gshegs su gsol lo// 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams dang / sngags rnams nyid la yang / sngags kyi dngos grub dang / dam tshig dang

33a5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po la/ rang gi rig pa'i tshogs sngags kyi'i hU~M rab byam gsungs par gyur to// na mo/ rgyas man+ta bud+yA na~M/ pra tiha ta sha swA na/ oM ni tri 'di ni nye bar spyod pa'i sgra can
33a6(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i rig pa las thams cad pa ste/ phyag rgya ni kha bye ba zhes pa gzigs las thams cad la sbyar bar bya'o// na maHsa man+ta br-ide d+ha nAM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa nAM/ oM ni rig pa 'di ni sdong bu can zhes bye ba spyod
33a7(rgyud): pa pa'i dge ba'i las thams cad byed pa ste/ phyag rgya ni bzang po'i gdan gyis/ gnod sbyin ma rnams 'gugs par byas pa la sU ri ro// na moHsa man+ta bud+ha naM/ a tsani tar+b+hu ta ru pa na oM ShA swA hA/ mkha'
33a8(rgyud): 'gro makun 'joms pa'i phyag rgya sbubs can yang dag sbyar/ byang chub sems dpa' bshad pa yi/ rig sngags pos can zhes bya/ sangs rgyas kun gyi padam nyid/ rab sngags lnga'i gzugs can mganam
33b1(rgyud): sa man bud ma~M/ a pra ti ha tag ta \u0f7f nI/ t+yad+ya thA/ oM bA de bya can zhes rgyan phyag rgya sung pal nyid ni/ dpal gyi dbadag nyidadi can la sbyar// gzugs ma 'chang ma'i lha mo ni/ myur du long spyod rab sprus
33b2(rgyud): pa'o// na maHsa man+ta bud d+ha naM/ a tsi t+yai d+h+yA ta rU si ni/ oM su ru swa hA// phyag rgya mdung dang yang dag ldan/ rigs rnams thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'o// na maHsa man+ta bud dA naM/ a tsi t+ya rgyu te
33b3(rgyud): nubi ni/ a trai re swA hA/ bsams pa'i sgrol ma ldan ma zhes/ rab sngags las rnams thams cad pa/ dbyug pa'i phyag rgyar yang dag ldan/ dgegs rnams 'joms bye'o ni sgyu
33b4(rgyud): na maHsarba bud d+ha ni/ a tsi ts+yai d+hu da/ ru bi Ni/ tad+ya thA/ oM bi'i k+ki ni swAhA// rigs pa snang ldan ma zhes bya/ 'jig rten thos cad dbang du byed// bde ba thams cad rab sbyin pa/ 
33b5(rgyud): pad ma'i phyag rgyas sbyar bar bye// na maHsa man+ta bu d+ha nAM/ a tsi t+yai d+hu ta rU pa nI/ tat+ye thA/ oM ba~M sre sa b+hI She/ bi rU ba ni ka hA kaM ha/ a br-i shA a bi shA/ sa ma oM ma nu smra
33b6(rgyud): rU ri ti/ Sha sahA// rig pa brtson 'grus chen mo ni// 'jig rten pas bstan pa ste// snying po phyag rgya mnyam pa nyid/ sems can thams cad 'bebs shing dge/ 'byung po kun la mchog
33b7(rgyud): sbyin ma/ sde tshogs zhes bya yang dag bsgrags/ na maHsa man+ta bud+d+hA naM/ a tsi t+yai d+hu ta rU pa nAM/ tad+ya thA/ oM swe te swe ba su swA hA/ pad ma'i gdan gyis rnam par dgod/ las rnams thams cad byed pa'o// 
33b8(rgyud): ni maHsa man+ta bud+ha naM/ a pra ti ha ta ga ti pre tsA ri Ni/ tad+ya thA aM shi/ rig pa 'di ni dpal tshon mo// 'jig rten mgon gyis bstan pa ste/ phyag rgya kha sbyor ldan pa yi/ rgyal chen po rab sbyin byed// 
34a1(rgyud): namaHsa man+ta bud+ha na~M/ sarbas ta bA ya pra dA yi ka/ tad+yathA/ oM a dza~M ti kA mA ra rU pa ni/ e hi mA/ gats+tsha ma kAr ya~M ku ru swA hA/ mi thub ma zhes rnam grags pa/ gzhon nu bdud rtsi las byung ba/ gang ba'i
34a2(rgyud): phyag rgyar ldan pa yi/ dag rnams cad bzlog par byed// na maHsa min bud+ha naM/ a tsi t+ya mU ru bi nI/ tad+ya thA/ oM dza ye swA hA/ oM dzi sing+ge/ bi dza ye swAhA/ a pA ra dzi te sa hA/ srings po ni zhes rnam grags pa// byang
34a3(rgyud): chub sems dpa'i rjes 'gro ba/ sa rnams mtha' dag yongs rgyu zhing / sems can rjes 'dzin byed pa/ mang po dum bu ru zhes grags/ 'di rnams kyi ni rjesu spyod// gru'i gzhon pa mnyam zhon nas/ rgya mtsho
34a4(rgyud): la ni nges par gnas/ khu tshur phyag rgya rnam par dgod// bsam pa thams cad yongs rdzogs byed// na maHsa man+ta bud+d+hA naM/ lo ga gA d+hi pa tI nAM/ tad+ya thA/ oM ku mu ri ma hA/ ku mA ri krI Ta krI Ta/ ma hA
34a5(rgyud): rAk+ta si/ bo d+hi sa d+ho nu dzA ta ma yu ra sa ne swa shwA/ sa ra shwA sA nir/ gri/ rak+ta gan+d+ha nu le pa na pr-i ye pr-i me/ kha kha khA hi khA hi/ hU~M nr-i tu ra ki ta ra pu kheSh+mArtsi te mU d+hi/ sa ma ya ma nu sma ra/ b+h+ra ma d+hA
34a6(rgyud): ma/ b+h+ra ma ya/ bA ma ya/ hu lu hu lu/ mA ba la~M pa sarba kA ra nA mi/ ku ru ku ru/ bi rtsi da ru pe d+ha tri ni/ tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha/ hUM hUM/ sarba bud+ha bu dzA te swA hA// / sems can rje su 'dzin byed pa'i// byang chub sems dpas be shad
34a7(rgyud): pa na/ sa rnams ma lus kun nas ni/ rnam pa drug tu rab tu g.yos// sems can kun la phan don dang // gdug pa'i sems can bzlog byed pa// bdag gi rigs pa rtag tu drag/ rtag tu srung ba yongs su grags
34a8(rgyud): bsrung ba ltos 'gro de nyid kyi// 'dzin pa'i mtshan mas legs par mtshan// snying rjes thugs ni rlan pa yis// byang chub sems dpa' de nas gsungs// byang chub sems dpa' bdag nyid che// byis pa rnams la phan
34b1(rgyud): don du// gang las sems can skyong gsungs pa// 'gro ba kun la rnam spyod ldan// phyag rgya dbyug pa'i srog shing ldan// bdag nyid chen pos sbyar nas ni// tshangs pa la sogs 'gugs byed na// mi rnams 'bras bu
34b2(rgyud): smos mi dgos// gzhon nu'i sem su ma lus pa'i// rtog pa 'di ni bsdus du nas su// srin po rnamasu rnam grags pa'i// rig sngagaso 'di na yang dag brtan// sems can rjes ba zung 'dod pa yi// byang chub
34b3(rgyud): sems dpa' de ltar bshad// yi ge g.yung zhes bya ba'i snying po ni// rig sngags 'di ni yang dag bshad// sems can kun la phani don du// nye bar long spyod 'gugs pa'i cho ga/ phyag rgya dbyug pa'i srog shing ni// rnam
34b4(rgyud): las rnams thams cad pa'o// oM hAM dza// rag sngags 'di ni mdor bsdus nas// mi rnams 'bras bu byed pa yin// na maHsa man+ta bu d+ha ne/ sa mo nA t+yo ti ta mu d+hi naM// oM bai kA ta kA ha hU~M phaT swA hA// nye ba'i
34b5(rgyud): snying po'o 'di yang ni/ phyag rgya gA ste yang dag ldan// de bzhin 'byu po 'gugs par byed// de bzhin bza' dang ma mor bcas ni/ thams cad phyag rgyas btab pa// dkon mchog 'bras bu bcas
34b6(rgyud): par 'gyur// 'byung po rnams ni rnam skrag byed// bdug pa bzhugs pa rnam par grol// 'di ni bcom ldan 'das ma 'phags ma sgrol ma'i pho nya mo chen mo las thams cad pa la ral pa gcig ma zhes bya ba
34b7(rgyud): rjesu sbrid ma/ la sa thams cad pa ste// bzlas pa tsam kho nas las thams cad byed do// 'byung po thams cad skrag par byed pa dang // 'gugs par byed pa dang / dbang du byed pa dang / rig pa 'dzin pa dang ngos/ 
34b8(rgyud): 'dod pa de thams cad rdzogs par byed do// na maHsa man+ta bud+ha naM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa na na~M/ tad+ya thA/ oM prah+ma su pra d+hA pra hA/ brtsa se shA nA~M ku ru swa hA/ sngags 'di tshangs pa chen po ste/ byang chub sems dpas
35a1(rgyud): bshad pa yin// 'byung po zhi ba rab tu thob// skad cig nyid la gsil bar 'gyur phyag rgya pad mas yang dag ldan// myur du dge legs thob par 'gyur// mngon spyod kyi ni las rnams las// srid srung gi
35a2(rgyud): ni rigs byed 'dod// 'di ni mdar bsdus brjod pa ste/ go cha 'di ni mdor bsdus pa'o// na maHsarba bud d+hA naM/ a pra ti ha ta shA sa nA nA~M/ tad+ya thA/ oM ga ru Da ba ha na tsa prA ni tsa dur b+hu dzaHhUM hU~M/ sa ma ya ma nu sA ra/ 
35a3(rgyud): bo d+hi sa two a dzA ba ya ti swA hA// byang chub sems dpa' bka' stsal pas// zhi ba'i don ni rgyu ru byed// 'byung po rnams ni nam 'jig byed// khyab 'jug kyis gzugs kyi lus can yin// phyag rgya'i 'khor lo yang dag
35a4(rgyud): ldan// brten po'i don ni myur du byed// gang 'di khyab 'jug rgyud du ni// chos gargyas par bstan pa de// sems can kun gyi sgrub bya de// byang chub sems dpa' sa bshad pa yin// na ma
35a5(rgyud): sa man+ta nu hAM nAM/ a pra ti ha ta sha sa na nAM/ tad+ya thA/ ma hA man+di/ saHb+hu tAd+hi ba ti/ gr-i Shi b+ha drA dza pra la badza tra ma ku Ta d+hA ri NAM sa tab+ha sA d+hA sa r-i ta/ mu d+hi ba aM phaT phaT/ pro d+hi sang+ga a dzA da ya ti
35a6(rgyud): swA hA/ sems can rnams la phan 'dod pas// sngags 'di dag gis rab tu brjod// mdung gi phyag rgya mnyam par lA ni// 'byung po thams cad rnam 'jig pa// 'di 'dra sngar bstan cho ga 'di// sems
35a7(rgyud): can sa stengs gnas pa la saston ni zhi ba'i rgyud du bstan// yon tan sna tshogs rgya che ba// zhi ba'i rgyun gyis kyang brjod do// na maHsa man+ta bud nAM/ a pra ti ha ta shA sA nA naM/ tad+ya thA/ oM shA kun pi ta ha @
35a8(rgyud): Na sha ka kha kha khA hi khA ti/ sa ma ya ma nu sma ra/ hU~M tiSh+Tha d+ho d+hi satwa A dz+nyA pa ti swA hA/ sngags 'di brtson 'grus chen po ste// nam mkha' lding zhes rnam par grogs/ gdul dka' 'dul ba rnams
35b1(rgyud): kyi mchog/ gdengs ka can gyi dug rnams 'joms// phyag rgya de dang yang dag ldan// phung mi khrol mi zad bcas pa 'joms// brtan dang g.yo ba'i dug rnam ni// gso bar byed pa the tsom med// gdul dka'
35b2(rgyud): bya'i sems can la rtse ba// byang chub sems dpa'i yang dog dka'// namakha' ldang gi gzugs ldang brjod// 'dab chags rgyal po 'od chen ldan// ji srid nam mkha' lding rgyud du// bstan pa'i cho ga rgyas de
35b3(rgyud): rnams// sems can kun la phan pa'i rgyur// bdag gis kyang ni brjod pa yin// mkha' lding mngon par brjod rgyud du// khro bo'i rgyal po ma bstan na// gdengs can dug ni gzhom pa'i phyir// 'dab chags gnas
35b4(rgyud): kyis rnam par rgyu// ji sbrid 'jig rten pa'i sngags// de rnams chog dper brjod pa// gdul bya'i sems can don dun/ 'di lta de ltar rnam par spyod// gang yang de bzhin gshegs sngags po
35b5(rgyud): dang // rdo rje pade ma'i rigs dag kyang de rnams cho ga rab 'byam 'dir snga ma kho nar sngon gsungs ya ni// ji ltar ma ma rnam mang po// byis pa 'bad pas bsrung byed pa// de bzhin byas mtha' blo can la
35b6(rgyud): nga ni rig sngags gzugs kyi rgyu// stobs bcu ldan pas sngon gsungs pa// da lta nga'i bsten pa yin// sngags rgyud don ni ma lus pa// rtogs pas rab gsungs 'od chen po// rgyal ba mchog gis gang gsungs
35b7(rgyud): dang // stobs bcu pa'i sras kyis gsungs// rmad byung bsam mi khyab gzugs can// spyan ras gzigs kyis gsungs pa'o// de nas yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po// spyan ras gzigs
35b8(rgyud): dbang phyug thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams der 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po de la kun du gzigs nas// dam tshig thams cad yang dag par skul bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
36a1(rgyud): par zhugs so// gang du ting nge 'dzin de la gnas pas sems can ma lus pa'i sgrub pa'i spyod pa'i yid// sems can thams cad la rab tu gnas par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' chen po snyoms
36a2(rgyud): par zhags ma thag tu thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor chen po gnas par// rnam par bkra ba'i phyag na rin po che'i snying po// brgyan bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab cing rmad du byung ba'i rnam par 'phrul
36a3(rgyud): pa// rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang / 'phags pa nyan thos dang / spyod pa la zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / sa bcu dang ldan pa sa bcu'i dbang phyug la gnas pa rnams kyis kyang / dkyil 'khor de
36a4(rgyud): bri ba 'am 'brir 'jug par mi nus pa// so so'i skye bor gyur pa'i sems can rnams kyis lha smos kyang ci dgos// 'phags pa'i dkyil 'khor bzang po de'i dam tshig sgrub pa'i gnas skabs la
36a5(rgyud): gnas pa/ byang chub sems dpa' chen pos gzigs nas// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang / 'phags pa nyan thos thams cad dang / byang chub sems
36a6(rgyud): dpa' sa bcu la rab tu gnas pa/ rgyal tshab du mngon par dbang skur zhing // dam tshig thob pa thams cad dang / spyod pa la zhugs pa rnams zag pa dang bcas pa dang / zag pa med pa'i sems can thams cad/ spyan ras
36a7(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug gis byin gyis brlangs kyis// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bas mo gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyu 'thun pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par gyis thugs las byung ba'i dkyil 'khor du rab
36a8(rgyud): tu zhags pa/ bdag nyid kyis yang dag par shes par gyur to// so so'i skye bo thams cad kyis de yid kyis dmigs par mi nus na bri bi'am/ 'brir 'jug pa lta smos kyang ci dgos// de nas yang byang chub sems dpa'
36b1(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshig la rjes su rab tu zhugs pa'i sems can de rnams la smras pa/ grogs po dag nyon cig 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
36b2(rgyud): dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis kyang 'da' bar mi bya ba'i dam tshig yin na/ sems can rnams dang / 'phags pa gzhan rnams kyis lha smos kyang ci dgos/ de nas yang sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje
36b3(rgyud): gsang ba'i bdag po la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ mi 'di las 'das pa'i dam tshig yid na/ sems can rnams dang / 'phags pa gzhan gyis lta smos kyang rtsi dgos// las byung ba ni nges par bstan to// mi
36b4(rgyud): rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa rnams yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa na yang gang du sems can rnams yang dag par rjesu zhugs nas/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i reg pa dang / sngags kyi dngos grub thams
36b5(rgyud): cad grub par 'gyur ba bshad par bya'o// de nas yang dgasang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rjes byang chub sems dpa' chen po spyan res gzig dbang phyug la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras gang da lta dus la bang
36b6(rgyud): par shes na gsungs shig gsungs shig/ shAkya seng ge 'jig rten mgon// yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i// mi rnams mchog gi sangs rgyas zhing / sems can sbeng khyod dkyil 'khor// mthong ba tsam gyis 'jig
36b7(rgyud): rten na// sngags kyi dngos grab rab ta ste// mi shes cho ga nyams pa 'am// dam tshig bdag por ma gyur na// tshangs pa bdag nyid chen pos kyang // rig sngags dngos grub mi 'gyur ro// sngags la mngon par mi brtson
36b8(rgyud): dang / dam tshig bstan pa ma mthong na// rnam pa du mar 'bar byas kyang // rig pa'i dngos grub ma 'gyur ro// dam tshig sbyor ba nyams pa ni// brgya byin gyis kyang rang 'bad las// rig pa'i dngos grub mi 'gyur na/ 
37a1(rgyud): sa stangs mi rnams smos ci dgos// dam tshig snyan chos ci ste shes// spyod ba'i las grub pa de// 'jig rten pa dang 'phags pa'i sngags// klags pa tsam gyis grub par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa'i
37a2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor du// rab zhugs las rnams thams cad byed// byang chub sems dpa'i' snyan pa la// de'i rigs pa'i dngos grub rtag/ de nas gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rjes// sems dpa' chen po la
37a3(rgyud): gsol btang par gyur to// kyai sems dpa' chen po// sems can rnams kyi don gyi phyir// dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mdor bsdus pas gsungs shig ces so// gsang ba'i bdag pos de skad ces smras
37a4(rgyud): pa dang // byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis// sems can gyi don gyi phyir dkyil 'khor cho ga gsungs so// dang po re shig
37a5(rgyud): 'phrul gyi zla ba phyed dam/ rnam pa can nam/ sa gtson gyi zla ba'i dkar po'i phyogs la/ rab tu sngags pa'i nyi ma dang / bza'abazang po ltas te/ rgyu skar dag pa dang / yang dag par
37a6(rgyud): ldan pa'i dkar po'i phyogs kyi chos gcig dang / zla ba nya ba 'am dus gzhan la dbyar gyi zla ba srengs/ snga dros rab tu gnas par bya'o// grong khyer chen po la sbyin pa 'am// gang du dkyil
37a7(rgyud): 'khor gyi slob dpon rang nyid gnas par gyur te/ rgya mtsho 'chu ba 'am/ chu klung la rten pa 'am/ rgya mtsho'i ngogs dang nye brar grong khyer chen po'i byang shar phyogs kyi char/ ha cang yang mi
37a8(rgyud): bar dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon song nas/ nyi ma bdun ni zla ba phyed du mtha' gcig tu snang ba'am/ nye bar byas nas so sor gnas par bya'o// gang gnas de rnams su yang gtsang ba'i/ 
37b1(rgyud): phyogs rdo ba dang / gyo mo dang / thal ba dang / sol ba dang / phub ma dang / thod pa dang / rus pa gnas pa dang bral ba// shin du sbyang bar byas pa'i sa phyogs su// srog chags med pa'i chu la/ ba byung lnga dang
37b2(rgyud): bsres pa'i tsin dan dang ga bur dang / gur gum gyi chus khro bo'i rgyal po sbrel mas non pa stong phrag brgyad kyis/ mngon par sngags pa des bcom ldan 'das ma'i phyag rgya chen mo dang / yang
37b3(rgyud): dag par ldan pas sa phyogs de la/ phyogs bzhi rnams su mngon par gtor zhing / steng dang 'og dang / thad ka dang / phyogs brel rnams su yang kan zhes gtor bar bya'o// de nas phyogs der
37b4(rgyud): kun nas gru bzhir/ khru bcu drug gam/ khru bcu gnyis sam/ khru brgyad bya ste/ de la chen po ni khru bcu drug go// ba ra ma ni khru bcu gnyis so// chung ngu ni khru brgyad do/ dkyil 'khor rnam pa gsum pa
37b5(rgyud): 'di/ thams cad gzigs pas gsungs pa yin// rgyal srid 'did phyir chen po de// bar ma long spyod 'phel bar byed// rlung ngu bsngags kyi dam tshig ni// las rnams kun byed ni nga yin
37b6(rgyud): de la yid la 'dod pa gang yang rung ba'i dkyil 'khor bri bar bya'o// de la sa'i phyogs der khru gnyis tsam nos la/ der rdzob dang / sol po dang / thal ba dang / rus pa dang / smug la sogs pa dang / sro
37b7(rgyud): chags kyi rigs rnam pa sna tshogs pa gal te mthong na sa'i phyogs gzhan du bskor bar bya'o// gnod pa med pa dang / nye bar 'tshe ba med pa der 'gyur ro// ri'i rtse mo dang chu klung gi ngogs dang / brgya mtshor
37b8(rgyud): 'bab pa'i chu klung chen po'i chu ngogs rnams su yang gang rab tu 'bad pa chen pos shin du so sor rtags te/ shin du gtsang shing srogs chags med par byas nas bri bar bya'o// sa'i phyogs der slar
38a1(rgyud): yang srog chags med pa'i tshul/ ba'i rnam lnga bsres pas chu klung gi 'gram gyis gtsang ma 'am/ grogs mkhar gyis gang du srog chags med pa'i sa des grang bar bya'o// bkang nas kyang leg
38a2(rgyud): par legs par gdungs te kun nas mnyam par byas la/ ji ltar 'dod pa'i dkyil 'khor rnam pa gsum bya'o// seng ldeng gi phung bu bzhi la khro bo'i rgyal po nyid kyis lan bdun mngon par bsngags
38a3(rgyud): par byas nas/ phyogs bzhi rnams su gdab par bya'o// mtshon sA lnga'i skud pa la khro bo'i snying pos lan bdun mngon par bsngags par byas nas/ kun nas dkyil 'khor grwa bzhi pa'i rnam pas bkri bar
38a4(rgyud): bya'o// de bzhin du dbus kyi gnas su nang du yang zur bzhi'i// rnam par bya'o// dbus kyi gnas na gnas pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon gyis rtsa ba'i reg pa'am/ rtsa ba'i snying po
38a5(rgyud): stong phrag brgyad bzlas par bya'o// phyag rgya chen po dang rtsa ba'i sngags kyis gtsug tor bcings te/ khro bo'i rtsa ba'i sdug kyis grogs bsrungs nas/ bdag nyid bsrung ba byas ste/ bzlas
38a6(rgyud): pa byed bzhin du phyi rol du phyung ste/ dkyil da 'khor la g.yas su bskor ba byas nas/ kha shar du phyogs te ku sha'i khres la nye bar 'dug nas sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad yid la byas
38a7(rgyud): te/ dkyil 'khor de kun nas gru bzhi'i rnam par bri bar bya'o// de nyid kyi phyi rol du ba rnam zhag gcog snang bar gnas pas grogs bzang po dang / rab tu gnas par bya'o// de la 'dir dkyil 'khor gyi slob
38a8(rgyud): dpon gyis sngon spyad pa rnams byas te/ rang gi rig pa dang sngags dang rgyud la mkhas pa'i mkhan pos sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir/ theg pa chen po la lhag par mos pas zhag gcig snang bar
38b1(rgyud): gnas pas grogs bzang po dang / yang dag par ldan pa stobs rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i bya ba mthong bas/ mtshon sna tshogs lnga'i phye ma bzhi po 'bar bas legs par spyad pa byas nas/ rtsa ba'i
38b2(rgyud): rig pa'i sngags dang snying pos mngon par sngags par phye ma dkyil 'khor dbus su gdab par bya'o// pha rol du yang rgyal mtshan dang ba dan sgreng ba dang / rta babs bzhis brtson pa dang / chu shing gi stong po
38b3(rgyud): 'bras bu'i tshogs kyis g.yur za zhing // kun nas 'bras bu'i tshogs kyis rab tu 'phyung bzhin pa dang / rnga bo che dang / rdza lnga dang / dung gi sgra nges par sgrogs pa'i sa'i phyogs su bsgrags par bya'o// 
38b4(rgyud): ngos bzhir rjes su 'thun pa'i bar du bsngags pa'i sgra chos mnyan par bya'o// phyogs bzhi rnams su theg pa chen po'i mdo sde'i gleg bam klag par bya'o// 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das
38b5(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol du phyini ma lho phyogs su klag par bya'o// 'phags pa zla ba'i sgron ma'i ting nge 'dzin nub phyogs su klag par bya'o// 'phags pa stong po bkod pa byang phyogs su'o// 
38b6(rgyud): 'phags pa gser 'od dam pa shar phyog su'o// de ltar glags bam klags pa po med na/ mdo sde bzhi po lhag par rtogs pa'i gang zag chos smra ba po la/ chos nyan pa'i phyir gsol ba btab par bya'o// 
38b7(rgyud): de nas dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon langs nas/ tsan dan dang ga pu ra dang / gur gum pa rnam par bsres pa'i me tog dkar po dri zhim pa la rtsa ba'i rig pa bzlas te/ dkyil 'khor de thams cad du gtsal du/ 
38b8(rgyud): bkram par bya'o// mngon par bkram nas phyi rol du phyung ste/ zhag bdun gyi bar du 'dod pa'i kha zas sten pa/ gnyis sam gsum byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa/ gso sbyong nye bar gnas pa/ snyen pa la gnas
39a1(rgyud): pa'i ri mo mkhan mkhas pa de gogs sam/ slob ma des khas blangs pa rab tu bzhes par bya'o// gang rtsa ba'i rig pa nyid kyis gtsug tor bcing bar byas nas/ de nas gser dang dngul dang / rin ze
39a2(rgyud): che rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i go 'phang rnam par bkra shing / 'bar la mdzes pa'i zangs kyi phye mo zhib mo so sor bzung nas/ long spyod chen po dang ldan zhing / chos dang ldan pa'i rgyal po rnams 'bri ru bzhag par bya'o// 
39a3(rgyud): dkyil 'khor mthong ba nyid las/ nges par byang chub la gzhol ba yin na/ sngags sgrub par byed pa lnga ci smos/ shAkya seng gi gas mchog myang 'das nas// sems na can bsod nams chung rnams la/ 'di lha'i long spyod
39a4(rgyud): ga la yod// cho ga 'di ni snyan par bya/ byang chub sems dpa' 'od chen lnga ni// skye bo bkren pa gzigs nas ni// nyung zhing mdor bsdus dkyil 'khor ni// mdor bsdus nas ni bstan pa yin/ 
39a5(rgyud): 'bras bu lu dang / thug po che'i phye ma shin du zhib mo mtshon sna lnga pa 'bar bas/ dkar po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / ljang kus kha dog du kha sbyar la/ sngar bzhag pa'i phye ma dkyil 'khor
39a6(rgyud): gyi slob dpon gyis blangs nas bcom ldan 'das ma'i phyag rgya chen po bcings te zartsa ba'i rig bzlas pas phye ma la phyag rgyas btab par bya'o// gzhan zhi ba grub pa po'i slob dpon gyis dkyil 'khor gyi phyi
39a7(rgyud): rol lho shar gyi phyogs las kyi cho ga me thab bya'o// khru gnyis kyi tshad la/ dbang su khru gang tsam gyi tshad la/ rlan dang yug tu pad ma'i ze ba rnam pa/ phyi rol pade ma'i rnam par shing pa la yam shing rnams
39a8(rgyud): me rab tu sbar te/ shing dpal 'bras kyi yam shing mtho gang tsam gyis tshad la/ rAn dang bcas pa zho dang sbrang rtse dang mar la rtogs pa rnams kyis/ rtsa ba'i snying pos bsam/ phyag rgya dang rtsa ba'i rig sngags kyis
39b1(rgyud): me lha spyan drang bar bya'o// spyan grangs nas kyang sngar brjod pa'i yi ge gcig pa nyid kyi rig pa 'am/ rtsa ba'i rig pa'i snying pos slar yang / brgya rtsa brgyad sbyin bsreg bya'o// de nas dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon gyis
39b2(rgyud): gtsug tor bcing zhing yod byang tshogs par byas nas/ bdag nyid dang ri mo mkhan ches mkhas pa 'am/ slob ma byed du bzhug go// de nas dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon gyis sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
39b3(rgyud): yid la byas nas sngar brjod pa'i gdug pa'i rigs pas gdug pa sreg go// thal mo sbyar bar byas nas sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dang

104b5(rgyud): shes rab thabs dang ldan pa ste// 'jig rten mi dge kun las 'das// dag par long spyod snyan pa can// sa dang sto bas ye shes bzod// pha rol phyin pa kun la mnga'// ting 'dzin mnyam par long skyod pa// rnam thar sgom pa/

130a3(rgyud): 'jigs par ma sems shig/ de nas rab tu cher bshad cing // 'brug chen sgra ltar sgrogs pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa zhal gsal bas// shar phyogs gzigs nas bka' stsal pa// kye ma gsang sngags mchog gi
130a4(rgyud): yul la sems can gti mug bsal ba'i phyir// seMs can rnams kyi bsod nams tshogs// shin du rgyas par 'byung bar 'gyur/ kye ma bsod nams cher rgyas pa'i// sems can rnams ni rab sbyang phyir// 
130a5(rgyud): dam pa sbyin pa grub pa'i gnas// 'jam pa klog gis rab tu bshad// la la gang zhig mnyam gzhag nas sdug bsngal thams cad sel ba yi// grub pa'i gzungs 'di bden pa 'am// yang na nyan na
130a6(rgyud): sems kyang rung // de'i don kun 'grub par 'gyur// sdug bsngal kun las thar par 'gyur// sdig pa thams cad rnam dag pa// de yis nges pa thob par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa chen dang // ring por mi thogs de

130a8(rgyud): dam pa de nyid kyang // gang zhig nges gnas 'don pa yi// sems can chen pos mi thogs par// tshe zad nas ni thob par 'gyur// sdig pa thams cad rnam dag dang // seMs can kun la stug pa dang // spros pa thams cad zhi ba yi

130b2(rgyud): pa'i dbyangs kyi mdun 'dug la// shin du dang brtse gcig tu// nang par langs nas su brjod pa// de la rigs sngags 'chang kun dang // de bzhin lha'i dbang po rnams// gnod sbyin srin po mang po rnamaso// rtag tu yang
130b3(rgyud): ni srung bar byed// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras kun dang // de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kun dang // de bzhin rdo rje'i mtshon ma tshang ba// de la nges par srung bar byed// de ni sangs rgyas skur zhugs shing // mnyam par gzhag par
130b4(rgyud): snang bar 'gyur// gnod sbyin lha'i bdag po rnams// dgegs dang log 'dren chen po rnams// dga' zhing bsam pa dag pa yis// rgyang ma nas ni phyag kyang 'tshal// de phyir dgegs ni dga' 'gyur bas// 'tshe bar
130b5(rgyud): byed kyang mi nus so// lan cig klags na tshangs chen dang / bsod nams mnyam pa thob par 'gyur// shes rab chen po gang zhig gis// nyin re mtshan mchog brjod byas na// dri ma med cing rab dag

131b2(rgyud): 'gro ba 'don par brtson pa po// nyi ma shar ba dang 'dra bar// zla ba nya dang byad kyi 'od// ltar bcas mi dang lha min rnams// 'di rnams thams cad gsal bar byed// 'jig rten gsum po g.yo bar
131b3(rgyud): byed gnod spyan srin po 'jigs par byed// phyag na ud pa la sngon po ste// ma 'jig ma 'jigs zhes brjod ma// bar snang du ni 'phar bar gnas// 'gro ba yang dag srung bar mdzad// mtshon
131b4(rgyud): cha'i bskal pa 'byung ba dang // 'jigs pa sna tshogs 'khrug don du// rgyal ba rnams kyis bdag bskyed de// ming rnams dran pa nyid kyis ni// sems can rtag tu bdag gis bsrungs// sna tshogs 'jig
131b5(rgyud): pa'i rgya mtsho las// sems can thams cad bdag gis sbrul// des na bdag la 'jig rten du// rgyal ba'i tshogs kyis sgrol mar sngags// thal mo sbyar bar byas nas ni// 
131b6(rgyud): gus dang bcas pas legs par gnas// gang zhig rgyal bas sngon skyugs pa'i// gsungs shig rgyal ba brgya rtsa brgyad// sa bcu'i dbang phyug mgan rnams dang // byang chub sems dpa'
131b7(rgyud): rab dga' ba'i// sdig spyong byed bsod nams dang // bkra shis grags pa 'phel bar byed// rter dang nor bu rnams 'phel byed cing // nad rnams thams cad rlag byed pa// dpal ldan shis las 'jog
131b8(rgyud): par byed// nad med che ni 'phel bar byed// sems can rnams la byams snyoms na// de dag dbyangs sgrogs thub chen pos// 'di skad zhus nas bcom ldan 'das// spyan ras gzigs dbang rab tu bshad/ 
132a1(rgyud): mchog rnams thams cad rab gzigs nas// 'di lta bu'i byams pas spros// phyag ni g.yas pas phyag thabs mdzad// bsod nams mtshan nyid ldan pa yi// 'di gsungs shes rab shin du che// 
132a2(rgyud): legs so legs so dka' thub che// sems can kun la gcig tu rtse// bskal pa chen po'i mi rnams nyon// mi rnams gang zhig 'don sgrogs pa// nor gyi dbang phyug yang dag 'gyur// nad rnams thams
132a3(rgyud): cad grol// dbang phyug kun dang yang dag ldan// dus min 'chi ba nges par sreg/ 'chi ba bde ba can 'gro ba// de rnams bdag gis bshad par bya// lha'i dge 'dun bdag la nyon// mi rnams gang zhig// 'di la

182b3(rgyud): shes kyi stobs rtul phod pa rnyes pa de yang snying po 'di'i byin rlabs kyis yin no// gcig sems can don rab rtson// sa gzhi la ni rnam par bzhugs// sems can rjes la phan 'dod pas// sprul pa rnams kyang 'gyed par mdzad// mcho

266b6(rgyud): rten dbang phyug thub pa che// rtse gsum thal pa'i dkyil 'khor can// mnga' bdag dbang phyug chen po ste// rten pa 'jig rten kun gyi rims// 'jig rten kun gyi pha ma lags// mnga' 'dzad sred med bu'i mchog/ 
266b7(rgyud): me dran rgyan can nor gyi lha gzhi ba'i bdag po spyan gsum pa// sna tshogs gzugs ston sems dpa' che/ 'gro la bar 'dzad 'gro ba'i 'gon// 'gro ba'i rtse 'o dbang phyug che// spyan la 'od zer 'phro ba 'o// 'gro
266b8(rgyud): ba kun gyi bdag po lags// dkyil 'khor rab tu 'bar ba can// gzugs 'dzes 'od b.rangs ri bo ste// sku rgyas ljags ni ring shing srab// zham ras pad ma'i 'dangs can bsal// shangs kyi dbyibs mtho ngag bshed thul// 
267a1(rgyud): dgra'i tsho gas las rgyal ba ste// sa la mkhas pa'i rdo rje 'dzin de/ mi dbang rdo rje dam pa 'dzin// nges par sbyor ba rdo rje'i blo// sum bcu rtsa gsum me'i bdag// drang srong chen po 'dren 'dzad pa// smra ba'i skyon
267a2(rgyud): mkhyen bgo bsha' 'dzad// dngos po rnam par 'jig pa'i thugs// shAkya seng ge seng ge che// shAkya sku tshe lo brgya pa// pad ma los byung pad mas spyan// mi thung gzugs can tshangs pa'i lha// zla ba'i 'od zer 'od zer che// 
267a3(rgyud): 'od zer rgyal po skar ma'i bdag/ sprin drug bdag po nyis gsum 'joms// rig pa gsum gyi skyabs gyi gsum pa/ khams gsum yis ni rnam par grol// sum bcu rtsa gsum grong khyer bdag/ sku sngo
267a4(rgyud): sku'i kho lag che/ kha dog gzugs parang grags pa che// jo bo'i gzugs can ni ba'i gzugs pa'i / ni mang rnam par gsum 'dzid pa// sbyin pa mkhyen sbyin pa phun sum tshogs/ rtog pa thams cad yongs
267a5(rgyud): ba// dpa'o rtsang slar spyod pa ste// snyengs pa mi mnga' brtson 'grus brtan// dus mkhyen tshad kyang mkhyen pa lags// sdig pa thams cad rnam par spangs// sems dpa' che zhing byams pa brnyes// sku lus che zhing
267a6(rgyud): stobs kyang che// tshangs pa'i dbyangs can dbyangs chen po// mi yi seng ge mi'i tha// thub pa'i rtse tho dam pa ste/ bar snang na mkha'i gos dang ldan// na mkha' stong pa gnas med par// skyon med nyon mongs thub pabo'o// 
267a7(rgyud): dgra las rgyal ba'i mtshon chen po// dgra bcom bdud rnams kun gyi gshed// zug rngu'i gnyen po zug tu 'byem// bdag med yongasu 'dzin mi mnga' dbang ba sems dpa' sems dpa' ched/ bder gshegs nyid
267a8(rgyud): 'khrungs bde gshegs nyid// pad ma snams la phyag 'tsha mo// bde bar gshegs pa thugs rje'i bdag/ spyan pas gzigs dang byug gi rje/ yon tan yang dag rgya mtsho'i mtshan// dus gsum dpa' su 'drod pa// mthong
267b1(rgyud): ba'i chos la mi zad paka 'jigs pa chen po brgyad las thar// dpal gyi rgyud las gsungs pa yi// dngos grub 'de ba myur du thob// 'gro ba kun la dmigs sems kyis// sangs rgyas phyag 'tshal zhes brjod pa'i// phyag na
267b2(rgyud): pad ma dpal gyis mtshan// rig pa'i rgyal po gus bton na// dge 'dun mchod rten 'du la'i sgo// 'phrog dang pha ma bsod pa dang // lung med gnas dang dus min blas/ gsang sngags gnyis pa'i sdig kun byang // 'phags pa spyan ras
267b3(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug la mtshan yang dag par bstod pa/ rdo rje phreng ba'i gzungs las byung ba rdzogaso// / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban de dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur te zhus nas rten la phab pa'o// phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa rdo rje 'dzin pa
267b4(rgyud): rnams kyis 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad kyis bstod pa/ de nas phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa rdo rje 'dzin pa de dag gis 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs la mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa 'di dag gis bstod do// 
267b5(rgyud): mad ma sems dpa' sems dpa' che// 'jig rten dbang po dbang phyug che// spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug brtan pa'i mchog/ rdo rje chos la phyag 'tshalo// chos kyi rgyal po dag pa ste/ sems dpa' che zhing blo gros che// pang ma'i bdag kyi
267b6(rgyud): pad ma che// phyag 'tshal pad ma'i mgon khyod la/ pad ma las 'khrungs pad ma'i 'od// pad ma dag par ba dag 'dza/ rdo rje pad ma pad ma'i skus/ phyag 'tshal pad ma'i mchog khyod la// snang ba chen po thams cad che// chen po dang mnyam dgongs pa me/ 
267b7(rgyud): dpa' chen po brtan pa che/ phyag 'tshal sems dpa' che khyod la// ses dpa' bsam mkhyen theg pa che/ rnal 'byor chen po po mes de che// bde rtsol bde 'jang dag pa'i don// phyag 'tshal pad ma rgyas khyod la// chos kyi de nyid dam pa'i don// dag bI
267b8(rgyud): chos de chos mchog 'dzin/ chos can rmad 'byung chos rab ldan// phyag 'tshal chos kyi tshogs khyod la// sangs rgyas sems dpa' sems dpa' chog/ chos kyi sos dpa' ses dpa' 'dzin/ seMs dpa' sos dpa' sos dpa' mchog/ sos dpal khyod la phyag 'tsham/ 
267b9(rgyud): spyan ngas gzigs dang dpa'i mchog/ mgon cheni rnam par gzigs pa'i rtso// 'jig rten spang 'jud 'jig rten don// phyag 'tshal 'jig rted mgon khyod la// 'jig rten yig yi ge ste/ yi ge mchog ste yige 'dras yige rang bzhin yige zabs// phyog/
